British Newspapers Comment on the War Situation

London: According to special dispatches published here today, most London newspapers are emphatically stating that the Norwegian war has reached a critical stage. The Times' editorial is titled "The Setback at Trondheim," and the Daily Telegraph says that anyone who studies the news of the Norwegian war will feel that the Allied war effort in that area has clearly been poor in recent days. Those who read the war reports in the newspapers in detail will understand this even more clearly. The Daily Herald asks the authorities to inform the public of the true situation of the war. The News Chronicle says that the British Army, Navy, and Air Force should urgently unify command so that they can achieve cooperation and make decisions quickly. The Times' editorial said that even if the German troops in Oslo and Trondheim have not yet met, it is now certain that it is only a matter of time. The Allied hope of quickly cutting off and annihilating the German troops in Trondheim has vanished, and the Allied forces fighting south of the city are in danger of being attacked from both sides and cut off. The most important task now is to defend a line that prevents German troops from invading the narrow strip of land stretching from the Swedish border to the North Sea and far into the Arctic Circle. The Allied forces must place a strong army and air force behind this line and make their strength sufficient to overcome the advantages initially held by the enemy and enable them to take the offensive against the enemy at an appropriate time and eliminate the enemy from Norwegian territory. At present, the procedure for expelling the invaders must take longer than originally expected when the navy initially won. However, people everywhere do not slacken in their efforts to save Norway from the abyss of suffering. The Daily Telegraph said that the main element of the Allied spiritual strength is that their governments all feel that they must not conceal the truth when the situation turns critical. In the history of various countries, no one is as determined in battle as Britain and France. The Norwegian war situation needs to be dealt with, lest the Allies lack determination. Today's situation is only a change in the second battlefield, and it has not developed as we hoped. The Daily Mail's editorial, based on the speech by Liberal Opposition leader Sinclair in the House of Commons yesterday, urging the government to take active action in the Norwegian war, said that today's decision must be made by the Allied Chiefs of Staff and cannot allow political reputation to influence this decision. (Reuters, 1st)

US Department of Commerce Releases Report: Japanese Economic Structure is Weak, Efuci Rejects "East Asia Bloc" Theory, Says Japan is Not Yet Economically Self-Sufficient 31

Washington: The US Department of Commerce released a report on the state of the Japanese economy in 1939, stating that Japan's economic structure is becoming increasingly weakened due to the war in China. Japan's focus on the war in China has had a detrimental impact on various other developments, such as economic instability, increased currency issuance, inflationary trends, lack of goods supply, reduced labor efficiency, and a large increase in national debt. Military production has increased industrial output by 5% compared to 1938, but the continued expansion of general industrial output has been hindered by insufficient supply of electricity and coal, lack of labor, reduced efficiency of machinery, and scarcity of key raw materials. The most satisfactory aspect of the Japanese economy is the improvement in agricultural conditions, such as the increase in the value of rice, wheat, and silk. However, prices have increased the cost of living for workers by 15.3% compared to 1938, while workers' earnings have only increased by 10% compared to 1938. In 1938, Japan's national debt increased by 30%, totaling US$5,595,000,000. In other words, it has more than doubled the debt amount before the war in China, and the debt absorption capacity has weakened, which is a cause for concern, as it is expected that Japan will issue US$1,500,000,000 worth of national debt in 1940. Since the outbreak of the European War, Japan has adopted a plan to crack down on speculation, regulate prices, and inspect shipping, but it is generally believed that Japan cannot enjoy all the benefits of the trade opportunities provided by the European War. (Reuters, 30th)

Tokyo: Efuci, a member of the Japanese House of Peers and former ambassador to the United States, who is known for his close ties to Britain and the United States, recently published an article in "Diplomatic Times" dismissing the theory of Japan, China, and "Manchukuo" forming an "East Asia Bloc" to seek economic self-sufficiency as "a daydream." He stated briefly that after carefully studying the Japanese economic life, it is known that Japan cannot survive economically without maintaining strong relations with foreign countries. (Havas, 30th)

Manila: The Philippine Congress today almost unanimously approved a new immigration law that limits the number of foreigners immigrating to the Philippines to 500 per year, passing the bill with 67 votes to 1. This new immigration law will have the greatest impact on Chinese and Japanese immigrants, as China and Japan previously had 2,000 to 3,000 people immigrating each year. However, this passed bill must be signed by President Quezon and approved by President Roosevelt before it can become law. (United Press, 2nd)

Mediterranean Situation Tense, British Far East Merchant Ships Change Routes, British Government Instructs All Ships to Detour Around the Cape of Good Hope, and Orders Prohibition of Royal Airplanes Stopping Overnight in Italy 36

London: According to news from Cairo, Egypt, the Egyptian government has taken precautionary measures due to the unstable situation in the Mediterranean. Shipping companies in Port Said and Suez have received notifications stating that British merchant ships that previously passed through the Suez Canal should now detour around the Atlantic Cape of Good Hope and enter the Indian Ocean. However, the British Naval Headquarters declared that traffic between ports along the Mediterranean coast is not subject to this measure. In addition, British merchant ships currently in the Indian Ocean have been ordered to detour around the Cape of Good Hope to return to their home country. (Havas, 1st)

London: After the British government implemented a precautionary plan in the Mediterranean, ships sailing from Britain to the East and the Far East will likely change their route around the Cape of Good Hope instead of loading large quantities of goods at Mediterranean ports. Even if British ships load goods for Naples, Italy, and Marseille, France, these goods may have to be transshipped by non-British merchant ships. Now the shipping companies of Port Said and the Suez Canal have received notifications that British ships will change their route around the Cape of Good Hope. However, it is heard that this precautionary plan will not cause all British ships to withdraw or change their route. Each ship's journey will be considered separately based on its circumstances, and the special needs of the goods it carries and the political situation at the time of departure must be considered. The British naval authorities in Cairo stated that British shipping within the Mediterranean will not be affected by the government's plans. Four days ago, British ships returning home north of Aden were allowed to enter the Mediterranean. However, since then, British ships in the Red Sea have been notified to detour around the Cape of Good Hope to return to Britain. A Reuters diplomatic correspondent learned from reliable sources that the British government's decision is an indication to Italy that the recent remarks made by Italian newspapers and spokespersons in the political circles are contrary to the spirit of the British-Italian Gentlemen's Agreement. It is particularly unfortunate that Italian newspapers suddenly changed their attitude when British-Italian commercial talks were about to take effect. One of the agreements being negotiated will stipulate that Italy builds ships for Britain in exchange for British coal. (Reuters, 2nd)

Paris: Regarding the British merchant ships stopping navigation in the Mediterranean Sea, well-informed sources here recently stated that the British government's adoption of this measure is to express that no matter what happens in the Mediterranean, Britain and France are prepared for any eventuality. Recently, Italy has adopted various methods to demonstrate anti-British and anti-French sentiment, so this British measure is necessary. Moreover, the Italian authorities allow the German Embassy in Italy to spread rumors that a pro-German figure in Italy, namely Farinacci, the former secretary-general of the Fascist Party, will succeed Ciano as Foreign Minister, and Bismarck, the counselor of the German Embassy in Italy, will succeed Mackensen as the ambassador to Italy. It is also said that the Italian government's appointment of Alfieri as ambassador to Germany yesterday is a prelude to the reorganization of the cabinet, so that pro-German figures can occupy important positions. Although these points are not substantial, Britain and France have to prepare for them in advance, because if Italy and Germany cooperate militarily, an incident is bound to occur in the Mediterranean. (Havas, 1st)

Rome: Imperial Airways of Britain, whose airmail planes fly to various destinations in the Near East and Middle East, has canceled Rome as a stop and will now stop in Athens, Greece, or Marseille, France. (Havas, 1st)

London: Reliable sources say that the measures the British government intends to take in the Mediterranean are purely precautionary. It is heard that the British government very much hopes that these measures are only temporary. The British government is only making these necessary precautions in view of the possible future situation in the Mediterranean. (Reuters, 2nd)

Rome: The British government took further precautionary measures yesterday, ordering Royal Air Force planes not to make their usual overnight stops in Italy. This order was issued following this week's order to British ships to stop sailing through the Mediterranean. It is widely believed that this order is the result of Italy's recent Jaron's implication that Italy might join Germany in the war. London's order prohibiting Royal Air Force planes from stopping in Italy was issued hours after British Chargé d'Affaires Sir Charles held talks with Italian Foreign Minister Ciano. (United Press, 2nd)

Rome: The Italian authorities seem to have decided to punish those who publicly sympathize with Britain and France. For example, a certain member of the Fascist Party was recently referred to disciplinary action by the party cadres for giving a speech praising Britain and France. Another journalist who had written articles criticizing Germany is currently being investigated by government authorities for punishment. (Havas, 30th)

London: There are rumors that Germany has concentrated a large army on the border of Yugoslavia, and Italy has also concentrated troops on the border between Albania and Yugoslavia. As for the Albanian border, the Yugoslav authorities have taken normal defensive measures due to the geographical situation. Italy Temporarily Will Not Abandon Non-Belligerent Status; Not a Combatant Nation; Mussolini Meets with US Ambassador; Near East Treaty Nations to Hold Meeting 37

Rome Mussolini met yesterday with US Ambassador Phillips. It is reported that the US Ambassador visited Mussolini due to the international situation. What they discussed is still unknown. However, according to US sources, this meeting gives the impression that Italy will not change its non-belligerent stance in the coming days. The British Chargé d'Affaires in Italy, Charles, met with Italian Foreign Minister Ciano for a long time yesterday. It is said that the conversation was quite harmonious. British figures in Rome believe that the decision of British ships not to travel through the Mediterranean does not reflect a change in the relationship between Britain and Italy or issues of common interest. Although the full meaning of this British decision is not fully understood by the Italians, they will certainly deeply understand the seriousness of the situation because of it. (Reuters, 2nd)

Washington The State Department recently stated that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has provided assurances to US Ambassador to Italy Phillips that Italy does not intend to abandon its non-belligerent status temporarily. There are no more than two reasons for this: one is that Britain decided to order all merchant ships to cease sailing in the Mediterranean, and the other is that Italy is not yet prepared, economically, militarily, and psychologically, to immediately assist Germany in the war. However, according to the US military and political circles, Prime Minister Mussolini still has the possibility of weighing his own national interests and changing his attitude at any time. If Italy decides to assist Germany in the war, its people, although generally unwilling to be enemies with Britain and France, will follow Prime Minister Mussolini's lead. Diplomatic circles say that at this time, Germany is exerting great pressure to request Italy, and strongly emphasizes the situation of the Norway-Czech war, which has proved that the German air force's power is above the British and French navies. Italy does not seem to be completely persuaded by this, and will continue to maintain an ambiguous attitude as far as it can, but is willing to support Germany for various indications that prove the Germany-Italy axis is solid and unbreakable. (Havas, 1st)

London Members of Parliament and those close to the British government here are pessimistic about the situation in the Mediterranean. They say that although it is rumored that Prime Minister Mussolini has provided assurances to the US Ambassador to Italy Phillips, no reliable news has been received from Rome to confirm this. Although Italy's attitude is still hesitant at this time, or even intends to "hesitate and retreat" because of Britain's warning (referring to the British merchant ships ceasing sailing in the Mediterranean), Italy's policy has already entered a path from which it is difficult to turn back. This is the view generally held by British authorities. Therefore, the government has already conducted talks with the Turkish government to deal with Italy's intervention in the Balkan Peninsula. (Havas, 1st)

Beauty Secrets (1) 43

Nowadays, there are fewer women who can be called "old" than before. Fifteen years ago, judging from a woman's appearance, 38 years old could be regarded as the end of youth and the beginning of middle age. But what about now? The transition period for women from youth to old age has almost been extended by ten years. Nowadays, women generally do not show signs of aging until they are 48 years old. In other words, take the current 18-year-old new movie star, Boni, for example, her youthful appearance can last for another 30 years. What about before? It was only 20 years. The "youth" of 30 years mentioned here for Ms. Boni refers to her private life. If it refers to her appearance in the films, with the modern various wonderful makeup techniques, lighting, and photography techniques, her youth can be maintained longer than in her private life. In terms of private life, not only Ms. Boni, but any charming 18-year-old girl can have 30 years of youth - ladies, if you want a beautiful appearance, please use Da Xi face powder; if you want white teeth, please use Da Xi toothpaste. (To be continued)

May Day Labor Day; Moscow Grand Parade; Military Parade Held in Red Square; Voroshilov Delivers Speech 44

Moscow On May Day Labor Day, an unprecedentedly grand parade and review was held here. The review ceremony began at noon in Red Square. Stalin, Molotov, Kaganovich, Kalinin, Andreyev, Mikoyan, Shvernik, Beria, and members of the Supreme Soviet of the Soviet Union, chairmen of various People's Committees, all ascended the podium of Lenin's Mausoleum. As for the representatives of the Moscow Soviet, Red Army and Navy commanders, Soviet heroes, diplomatic corps personnel, and foreign journalists, they were seated on another platform. The reviewed troops were commanded by Soviet Marshal Budyonny, and the People's Commissar of Defense Voroshilov stood in front of the troops and delivered a speech, saying,

"Currently, only the Soviet people can celebrate this Labor Day with enthusiasm. The Soviet people are proud of the achievements of Soviet socialism. At the same time, they are particularly satisfied that they have not been involved in the Second Imperialist War."

"To this day, the people of capitalist countries must more deeply recognize the difference between capitalist and Soviet countries. Under the leadership of Lenin, Stalin's party, and the great Stalin, 183 million Soviet people are working hard to build their socialist life. The Soviet Union does not want to join the war, but is ready to fight at any time."

The defeat of the Finnish Defense Forces and the destruction of the Mannerheim Line have proven the strength of our people and the glory and bravery of the Red Army.

"The current international situation is extremely complicated. The Second Imperialist War has gradually expanded. Agitators are now trying to drag us into this bloody massacre, and even attack our territory when the opportunity arises. Therefore, we must be ready to deal with everything at any time. We must redouble our efforts to strengthen the defense of our motherland and consolidate the strength of the Red Army and Navy. We must complete this task in the spirit of Bolshevism, and the completion of this task is guaranteed by the will of our 183 million people and the wise Lenin-Stalin Party."

The troops were praised by the guests for their neat steps during the review. At the same time, the Red Army and Navy commanders also passed the review platform to pay tribute to Stalin and his comrades. Behind these commanders were students and instructors from military academies.

The most noteworthy thing was the infantry's procession. Their neat steps and majestic spirit received unanimous praise. At this time, armed members of the laboring masses entered the field. They were textile workers, railway employees, scientists, and artists, carrying long guns and full of spirit, indicating that they were ready to rise up and defend their motherland at any time.

More than 600 aircraft perform new tactics

After the infantry were cavalry, machine gun teams, artillery teams, and motorcycle teams. After that, the air defense forces also held a demonstration, showing the thoroughness of the Soviet Union's air defense. The Red Army's new weapons were also shown during the review. The various artillery pieces showed great power when they passed by. The orchestra, with more than 1,000 people, had a majestic and moving tone. Tank and armored vehicle teams galloped through Red Square, attracting attention. There were as many tanks as carp crossing the river. The large Red Square could hardly accommodate them. Three aircraft performed in the sky at this time, with novel postures never seen before. At the same time, various aircraft, in teams of nine, performed in the sky over Moscow. The fighters and bombers that were performed at that time were very new, and they were as fast as thunder during the performance, and the audience was overwhelmed. A total of 634 aircraft participated in the performance. (TASS, 1st)

Moscow After the Red Army was reviewed in Red Square on Labor Day, the laboring masses entered the field one after another, holding slogans and flags, and held a grand parade. First were the factories and cultural figures, followed by athletes. They all paid tribute to Stalin and his comrades, and cheered for their leaders, with voices shaking the sky. In the slogans and slogans, they expressed their respect for the heroic Red Army and were ready to deal with everything. Slogans were everywhere, fully supporting the Soviet Union's neutral policy.

The parade of the laboring masses lasted for four hours, showing the political unity of the Soviet people and their support for the party and Stalin. (TASS, 1st)

Soviet Defense Commissar Issues Proclamation on May Day

Moscow Soviet Defense Commissar Voroshilov issued a proclamation today for Labor Day, saying,

"Today, our people celebrate May 1st, which is a memorial to review the achievements of our laboring masses. This year, the Soviet Union should celebrate this memorial day in a solemn manner, because in addition to the great achievements in socialist culture and peaceful work, the Soviet Red Army has also added glorious victories to the motherland."

Although Britain and France attempted to drag us into the European war, thanks to the wise policies of the government and the party under Stalin's leadership, our country was fortunate not to be affected. The war waged by the British and French groups against Germany has now tended to expand, and new countries have been involved in the war. At the same time, in the Far East, the war is also continuing. Regarding our country's foreign policy, it has been explained by our head of state Molotov in the Supreme Soviet of the Soviet Union, and has been approved by the Supreme Soviet. This Bolshevik foreign policy is very clear. Its main purpose is to guarantee the peace of all countries and the security of our country. This policy is guaranteed by our country's treaties with various countries, and is also supported by our 183,000,000 people and armed comrades. Last autumn, the Finnish government became a plaything of "powerful" protectors. Not only did it fail to sign a friendship treaty with our country, but it also waged war against us.

The Soviet government immediately took steps to protect Leningrad and our northwestern border. As a result, the Finnish Defense Forces have been fatally struck by the Leningrad Military District troops, and the so-called Mannerheim Line has also been destroyed. The Mannerheim Line was built by imperialist experts, engineers, and staff, and was a military base for preparing to attack the Soviet Union.

The Mannerheim Line and the Maginot and Siegfried Lines are the same. The line is built with hundreds of strong bunkers, machine guns, artillery, tunnels, landmine traps, tank vehicle nets, and various other obstacles. War instigators believed that the line was an impregnable fortress, and that any army would be defeated, but under the serious blow of the Leningrad District troops, it was eventually shattered. Stalin once said that as far as the Bolshevik Party is concerned, there is no impregnable fortress in the world, and this statement has now been proven.

In this war, Soviet Red Army officers and political personnel have not only fully demonstrated the morale of the Red Army and the greatness of Soviet military equipment, but have also proven that the Red Army can make good use of its weapons in any environment. In addition, in addition to defeating the Finnish army, the Red Army has also defeated the imperialist armed forces that attempted to turn the Finnish war into a world war. The war in recent days has given the Red Army new experience in war. We should study this new experience, correct our shortcomings, and continue to enhance our strengths. Bolsheviks do not have the habit of sticking to the old ways. We should not feel complacent about our victories. The times are progressing, therefore, the Red Army must continue to enhance its strength, and should strive for perfection in terms of military knowledge.

Imperialist war instigators must still threaten our country with war, therefore, we should be prepared at any time and improve our combat power to repel any enemy that attacks our motherland. Also, Soviet Navy Commander Kuznetsov issued a proclamation, pointing out the political significance of Labor Day and the achievements of the Soviet Union in recent years. The text reads, "The Soviet Baltic and Northern Fleets have completed their tasks at the same time as the Red Army, defeating the Finnish Defense Forces, and the government has commended the naval achievements." (TASS, 1st)

The Situation in Macau is Very Tense 48

Hong Kong The situation in Macau is very tense. Although the Portuguese and Japanese authorities have repeatedly denied it, it has been confirmed by visitors from Macau. Last week, two Macau Indian policemen were shot dead by soldiers holding Japanese flags on Lapa Island. Another Indian policeman and a Portuguese policeman from Shanghai were injured. Last Sunday, a motor ship loaded with armed Japanese soldiers landed on the coast of Macau, causing great panic among the residents. The Japanese soldiers went directly to the business center of Macau to enter large hotels to gamble on fan-tan. Nearby Chinese merchants, banks, and shops immediately closed their doors. The Portuguese military police authorities rushed to send armed military police to guard important locations until the Japanese soldiers left in the evening. Although no accidents occurred, it has left a very bad impression on the residents. It is heard that many wealthy Chinese in Macau intend to move to Hong Kong, so the demand for Hong Kong dollars is extremely high, resulting in a sharp drop in Chinese currency. (Reuters, 1st)

Japanese Warships Rampage in Various Beaches of Dongting Lake 53

Changde In the past week, Japanese warships have frequently sailed to various isles and beaches in Dongting Lake to harass. (1) At 8 am on the 24th, many Japanese ships sailed from Yueyang to the waters near Yuelang Island (southwest of Lujiao) to scout, and fired machine guns at the shore. After the Chinese army counterattacked, they retreated north. At 3 pm, Japanese ships came in groups again. After the Chinese army along the lake discovered them, they immediately launched a fierce attack. The Japanese ships retreated quickly. (2) At 7 am on the 26th, Yueyang Japanese dispatched troops to sail in small boats to harass the Lushixi Bay area on the shore, and were repelled by the Chinese army. (3) On the 17th, three Japanese warships and more than ten motorboats were found in the Lujiao market area, and four Japanese planes flew low to cover them. Japanese soldiers on the ships forcibly landed nearby. The Chinese army took advantage of their departure from the ships to launch a surprise attack. The Japanese soldiers fell into the water one after another. Two Japanese warships and several Japanese motorboats were hit and damaged. The remaining soldiers boarded the ships and retreated. At 10 am on the same day, three Japanese motorboats were also found cruising on the lake surface east of Huanghuatan, and left about half an hour later. (4) At noon on the 28th, three Japanese warships and three motorboats came to the lake surface several miles east of Yuelang Island, and were also repelled by the Chinese army. (1st)

Ministry of Education Specially Establishes National Music Education College; Assigns Preparatory Committee; Scheduled to Be Established During Summer Vacation 54

(Chongqing, 2nd) In order to promote music education, the Ministry of Education has specially established the National Music Education College. Overview of Adult Education Implementation in Guizhou Province (5) 59

(7) Implementation Situation

(1) Establishment of Adult Classes: According to the results of a renewed survey, there are 2,798,875 adults in the province who should be enrolled in school. According to the prescribed number of people per class, 63,395 adult classes must be set up throughout the province. In addition to setting up adult classes in basic schools at all levels, secondary schools and above, and other cultural and industrial organizations, each county also sets up at least two demonstration adult classes in specially designated secondary schools or central basic schools with excellent performance, as a demonstration for general adult classes.

As for the establishment of adult classes for special ethnic groups in various counties, it is handled in accordance with the "Provisional Measures for Adult Education for Ethnic Groups in Guangxi Province." It is jointly handled by teachers of national basic schools in the villages and streets where they are located, and one class is conducted per period until it is completed.

(2) Phased Implementation: The implementation of adult education is limited by teachers and textbooks, and for the convenience of supervision, the adult classes in the province are generally divided into four phases. However, the environment in each county is very different, and those that are divided into districts and phases each month are handled separately. Generally speaking, each county can complete the process as scheduled according to the predetermined progress. The number of adult classes and students in each phase in the province is as follows: (Phase 1) 662,217 people enrolled, 18,172 classes, 9,086 teachers, 531,383 graduates, started on March 16th and ended on May 15th; (Phase 2) 657,665 people enrolled, 18,165 classes, 9,083 teachers, 520,14 people graduated, started on June and ended on July 31st; (Phase 3) 632,863 people enrolled, 17,196 classes, 8,598 teachers, started on August 16th and ended on October 15th; (Phase 4) 522,435 people enrolled, 14,401 classes, 7,201 teachers, started on November 1st and ended on December 21st. The total number of enrollments above is 2,474,180, 67,934 classes, and 10,550 teachers, starting from March 16th and ending on December 30th. (Note: (1) The total number of teachers refers to the total number of teachers transferred from various counties and who have received short-term training. (2) The number of graduates in the 2nd and 4th phases is temporarily missing because the war in southern Guangxi affected the reporting of various counties.

(3) Work Review: In order to provide practical problems with the experience of adult education workers, and to increase educational efficiency with the purpose of brainstorming ideas, the "Measures for Phased Discussion Meeting of Various Adult Education Programs" are formulated, stipulating that each county shall convene local adult class teachers and county adult education supervisors within one week after the end of each adult class session to hold discussion meetings. Adult class teachers must submit work reports before the meeting as a reference for studying problems. The discussion matters include the equipment of adult classes, student enrollment and organization, curriculum, teaching materials, teaching, training, continuing education, and adult education for special ethnic groups, and the work of the next adult class is planned. Adult education in each county has made much progress after each review meeting. The problems of the first and second phases of adult classes are rarely present in the third and fourth phases, and the results of the third and fourth phases are far better than the first and second phases. The effectiveness of the review meeting can be seen in general.

Foreign Exchange Fluctuations Drastically Yesterday, Government Decides to Stabilize Currency, Stabilization Fund to Be Significantly Increased, US Loan to China Highly Likely, Japanese Conspiracy Fails, Speculators Also Profitless 69

When Dr. Monroe, a leader of the American business community in Shanghai, visited Shanghai on the 26th and 27th, he reviewed China's financial problems. Fearing that American businesses would be excluded from trade with China in North China, he was deeply concerned that the Japanese would imitate the measures implemented in Tianjin in Shanghai and use the worthless paper of the pseudo "Central Bank" as a tool to attack the legal tender. On the 30th of last month, he sent a telegram to Secretary of State Hull, suggesting that a huge loan be given to China to stabilize China's currency system and consolidate China's finances. This would not only protect American trade with China, but also boost the morale of the Chinese people and strengthen China's position. Dr. Monroe is preparing to lobby after returning to the United States to make it happen. This news spread, and there were rumors that Britain would no longer maintain the stabilization fund, and that the value of Chinese currency would fall in the future, so the United States would come out to maintain it. Until yesterday, the Shanghai foreign exchange market experienced drastic changes and the situation was extremely chaotic. It cannot be said that this drastic change was caused by the above-mentioned proposal, but the turmoil happened at this time, which should be the most important issue for Chinese and foreign people. The information obtained from yesterday's investigation is recorded below:

Stabilization Committee Continues to Maintain 70

Yesterday afternoon, the leaders of the banking community in this city received a private telegram from Hong Kong. According to people close to the financial authorities, the Central Government has always maintained the exchange rate of legal tender in Shanghai through the Stabilization Fund Committee. The two previous contractions of the foreign exchange black market were to combat Japanese conspiracies and crack down on speculative activities. Now the Central Government has decided to increase the foreign exchange stabilization fund, and it is expected that the foreign exchange market in Shanghai will stabilize. The black market exchange rate of legal tender has been very stable for several months, and recently there has been a loosening trend. It is heard that the Central Government intends to increase the Shanghai Fund by 5 million pounds in British currency and 7.8 million US dollars. If this news is true, then this suspension of supply is purely to crush the positions of speculators, and foreign exchange can be gradually released, while those who blindly speculate will only suffer the consequences.

United States Will Never Stand Idly By 71

According to an economic expert yesterday, the center of gravity of American interests in China is in Shanghai. Whether it is investment or trade, almost all of it is concentrated in Shanghai. Since Japan has controlled trade in North China, American businesses have no room for development in Tianjin. Shanghai is the main market for American goods. At present, sales of American goods in Shanghai account for 75% of American exports to China, and exports from Shanghai to the United States also account for more than 80% of the country's goods shipped to the United States. Unless the United States is willing to withdraw from the Chinese market, it will never allow the Japanese to manipulate it. The reason why the Japanese have been hesitant to destroy the legal tender and abuse control is that they know there are concerns.

Financial Market Yesterday Morning, Suddenly Unprecedented Chaos 72

Crazy Rise Within Two Hours

The English-language Greater America Evening News said that the exchange rate of legal tender fell sharply this morning (2nd). Yesterday (1st), the average exchange rate of legal tender against the US dollar was 16.5 yuan, but this morning it rose to 20.75 yuan within two hours. It only recovered slightly an hour before noon. The closing price at noon was 20 yuan in legal tender, equivalent to one US dollar. When the market opened this morning, the exchange rate between Shanghai and New York was 5.9625 yuan. There were only buyers and no sellers. Then the news that HSBC and Markali refused to sell foreign exchange spread throughout the city. Obviously, the Sino-British Stabilization Fund had stopped interfering in the Shanghai black market. Buyers' bids became higher and higher, causing the US exchange rate to shrink to 4.9375 yuan for spot goods and 4.6875 yuan for May futures. Some sellers then dumped their goods, but it is not known whether their dumping was due to the resumption of work by the Stabilization Fund. The buying trend in the market is still strong, but it is more cautious. By noon, the New York exchange rate had eased slightly, and the closing price was 5.125 yuan for spot goods and 5 yuan for May futures. The future of the market in the afternoon is unpredictable. As the US exchange rate has shrunk unprecedentedly, the British exchange rate has also shrunk to 3.5 pence, which is the lowest record in August last year.

Yen Exchange Rate Also Fell Simultaneously

The banking community in this city was strongly impressed by the fall in the exchange rate of the Japanese yen against the legal tender. At noon, 100 Japanese yen could still be purchased for 125 yuan in legal tender. 100 yuan of Japanese military currency only required 124 yuan of legal tender to be purchased. Therefore, the yen exchange rate in this city is "only slightly more than one-quarter of the official exchange rate in Tokyo." The development of the foreign exchange market this morning immediately had a strong impact on other markets. The Stabilization Fund or its representative bank did not explain the reason for suddenly withdrawing support from the foreign exchange market, causing various rumors to arise, and reliable information could not be obtained. The saying that the United States is about to assist the legal tender has not been confirmed, but it is generally believed that the United States will take measures, at least to assist, the legal tender traded within "Free China."

Gold Price Reaches Unprecedented Peak

Cash was also greatly affected yesterday, creating a crazy surge. The market opened yesterday morning with an astonishing phenomenon, rising to 6,800 yuan, a sudden jump of 1,072 yuan compared to the closing price of 5,728 yuan the day before. However, it soon fell sharply by 800 yuan, followed by a flying rise to an unprecedented peak of 7,000 yuan. Afterwards, it fell again to 6,300 yuan, and when the market closed at noon, it fell back to 6,260 yuan. Decorative gold was only 100 yuan higher, at 650 yuan.

Serious Situation Created, Various Rumors from Outside, Financial Community Says Two Major Reasons 73

Yesterday, the black market situation in this city's financial sector was extremely tense. The financial community believes that the creation of this phenomenon is based on two important reasons: (1) Because HSBC and Markali banks stopped supplying foreign exchange for a time to prevent the Japanese from engaging in large-scale arbitrage, there were doubts about the Stabilization Fund. (2) In view of the sharp increase in Shanghai Customs' trade deficit in the past few months, according to investigations, the national trade deficit in the first quarter of this year was 900 million yuan calculated at the black market exchange rate, and 250 million yuan in Shanghai alone, which led to a sharp increase in the demand for foreign exchange in Shanghai. (The saying that there is a trade surplus is calculated based on the legal exchange rate and does not have accurate figures).

External Speculation Absolutely Unreliable

In the market yesterday morning, there was another rumor that the reason why the black exchange rate had undergone drastic changes and suddenly tightened was that it was rumored that the pseudo "Central Bank" was about to be established. However, according to reliable sources yesterday, this news is extremely difficult to confirm, and the authoritative side also stated that even so, its impact on the exchange market would not be so great. The reason why the exchange market suddenly tightened was mostly due to the sharp increase in this city's trade deficit. According to the banking community, the need for foreign exchange in this city has suddenly increased in the past few months, and the reason for this increase is nothing more than the sharp increase in the quantity of imported goods in this city. The sharp increase in the quantity of imported goods is enough to make Chinese and foreign merchants in this city buy and pay for the goods no matter how high the exchange rate rises.

Japanese Buying Large Amounts of Foreign Exchange

In addition, the banking community also stated that in addition to the increased demand for foreign exchange in this city, the amount of foreign exchange that the Japanese have purchased with legal tender in the past few months is also quite alarming. In the past, the Japanese used customs revenue as a source of arbitrage for foreign exchange. According to estimates by the general public, the Japanese exchanged tens of millions of yuan of legal tender for foreign exchange in the past four months. This may be another reason for the sudden tightening of the exchange market.

New York British Exchange Rate Also Fell

Reuters, New York, 1st. Due to the uncertainty of the Norwegian situation and Britain's decision to reroute cargo ships around the Cape of Good Hope, the New York British exchange rate fell successively this morning. The pound opened at 3.485 yuan and recovered slightly at 3.49625 yuan at the close. Yesterday's closing price was 3.50875 yuan. The French franc opened at 1.98375 yuan and closed at 1.98125 yuan. Yesterday's closing price was 1.99 yuan. Foreign public bonds were sold quite actively, and the price of Italian public bonds fell due to the increased tension between Britain and Italy.

International Relief Society Ends Operations, Reception Center Closed, Donations No Longer Accepted 74

The Shanghai International Relief Society issued a public notice to all sectors yesterday, stating that the society's work of providing relief to refugees will soon be three years old. A total of six large-scale reception centers, two refugee hospitals, one street children's education center, and one refugee children's middle school have been established successively, accommodating a total of more than 100,000 people. Fortunately, people from all walks of life have been compassionate and have provided continuous assistance. The Standing Committee of the Society has previously decided to close the affiliated reception centers on April 30. All refugees, except for the elderly, weak, disabled, and those who have no one to rely on, will be resettled separately, and the rest will be given generous severance pay. The severance procedures have been completed, and from May 1, the Society will no longer accept donations from all sectors. It is also scheduled that on June 1, the Society's head office will move to the Huayang Yizhen Society on the fourth floor of No. 97 Renji Road to handle the closing, compile an annual report, and distribute it to all sectors for credibility. This is to inform you and express our gratitude.

The Stability of the Legal Tender and the Abundance of the Stabilization Fund 75

The Determination to Maintain the Currency System Was Already in Place

The Chinese government has always held the greatest determination to maintain the stability of the currency system and foreign exchange. Now, more than two years into the war of resistance, the legal foreign exchange rate remains as before, namely one shilling, two and a half pence for the British pound and thirty yuan for the U.S. dollar. The government still provides as much as possible for the legitimate needs of various industries. As for the black market exchange rate in Shanghai, the Exchange Stabilization Fund Association also provides appropriate maintenance, and does not stop supply due to the manipulation of speculators. This situation has been proven by facts for some time. The fund itself is still substantial, and the claim that it has been used up is purely unfounded.

Lower Exchange Rates Benefit Exports

According to general observations, the sudden tightening of the black market exchange rate seems to be closely related to the future of the legal tender. It is believed that the future of the legal tender can be determined by the drastic changes in the black market exchange rate. The most significant reason for the sudden tightening of the black market exchange rate is the rumor that problems have occurred with the Exchange Stabilization Fund. The so-called Stabilization Fund is intended to facilitate foreign trade, but in the end it has led some people to profit from it, resulting in the current chaotic and bad situation. According to authoritative sources, it is believed that the value of Chinese currency is currently developing along natural lines. If we take this as an observation point, it is closely related to foreign trade. Considering the sharp increase in imports over the past few months, the trend created by this, when calculated nationwide, has become a phenomenon of continuous increase. Therefore, the decline in the value of Chinese currency seems difficult to prevent by human effort, but it is not entirely unfavorable to China's overall foreign trade, because the fall in the exchange rate can reduce imports of foreign goods and increase exports of domestic goods, and the two may still tend towards equilibrium in the future.

The Stabilization Fund Remains Abundant

In addition, we must also pay attention to the fact that the policy of the so-called Stabilization Fund is not to prescribe a fixed exchange rate for the Chinese legal tender, so as to avoid excessive expenditure of the Stabilization Fund. However, if we think that the Stabilization Fund provided by the two major British banks has a fixed amount, then this judgment is actually a misunderstanding. This can be proven by the recent analysis report of the two banks, because the two banks can also obtain profits from selling and buying in the foreign exchange market. Therefore, we can assert that the Stabilization Fund will not only not be exhausted, but the two banks can continue to find ways to maintain or expand its amount.

Speculators Will Find It Difficult to Profit

The foreign exchange transactions in April have already been settled. It is reported that speculators have entered into between seven and eight million U.S. dollars in May futures. Judging from the current operation of the Stabilization Fund, the long side has no profit to make at present, and the same will be true in the future. Most of the U.S. dollars entered were purchased when the exchange rate was low, and in the future they will have to grit their teeth and sell them off, or be willing to pay a fee to exchange them for June futures, hoping that the environment will be favorable at that time. These speculators believe that the exchange market will only shrink and not rise, so the news of the increase in the Stabilization Fund has destroyed their hopes.

Today's May Third Memorial: Citizens are Encouraged to Strive, Strengthen their Belief in Resistance and Nation-Building, Unite as One, and Practice Spiritual Mobilization, Saving and Disaster Relief Through Thrift 76

Today is the 12th anniversary of the Jinan Massacre and the martyrdom of Cai Gongshi. All sectors of the city, due to the special circumstances and in accordance with the central government's regulations, will not engage in extravagant activities, but will commemorate this painful massacre spiritually. In order to support the resistance and build the nation, they will practice spiritual mobilization, saving and disaster relief through thrift. Because on the "May 1st" Labor Day, a large number of leaflets supporting resistance and nation-building and patriotism were found in the Hongkou, Zhabei, and Nanshi districts, the Japanese sent a large number of artillery vehicles and armored vehicles to patrol the areas separately from 10:00 a.m. yesterday. Japanese and puppet police have been added to the bridges in Hongkou District and the iron gates in Nanshi District, and they have conducted extensive searches of pedestrians and vehicles. Therefore, in recent days, there have been very few people traveling to and from these areas.

A Letter from the Shanghai Municipal Party Department to Citizens

The Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang issued a letter to the citizens regarding the "May 3rd" Massacre, saying: Time flies, and May 3rd has arrived again. Twelve years ago, around this day, the Japanese warlords, in order to prevent the Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army, launched a massacre in Jinan. The invaders painstakingly planned to swallow China in one gulp. From the Sino-Japanese War to the present, they have not hesitated to create a series of bloody debts, also wanting to swallow China. "If China does not perish, aggression will not stop." This sentence speaks to the hearts of the Japanese warlords, and also explains the causes of their launching various massacres and incidents. In the past two years and ten months, for the freedom and liberation of the nation, for the survival of the motherland, for not wanting to be the descendants of a conquered nation, and for liquidating the long-unpaid blood debts of the Japanese, under the leadership of President Chiang, we have launched an unprecedented all-out war of resistance. Today, the war of resistance has tied down the Japanese, and their fighting spirit has declined. Panic and war-weariness are everywhere in the country. These are precisely symbols of the invaders shooting themselves in the foot and embarking on a dead end. Because the invaders have no way to end the war militarily, with the end of the war far off, they use puppet organizations to divide the forces of resistance. This is their last card, which they have always regarded as a rare commodity. Little do they know that they have bought fake medicine in the gourd, and hoping that it will work is simply wishful thinking. Dear citizens, the Japanese war of aggression is on the eve of collapse, and its last card has also appeared. At the same time, the all-out war of resistance under the leadership of President Chiang, after two years and ten months of tempering, has revealed the glimmer of victory. The facts tell us that the last five minutes of struggle are the key to determining the overall situation. From now on, we must strengthen unity and strengthen resistance and nation-building in order to strive for the freedom and liberation of the nation and the country. Only by strengthening unity and strengthening resistance and nation-building can we crush aggression and liquidate decades of blood debts.

The Chinese Army on the Qinghu Road Achieved Significant Victory. Most of the Japanese Troops in the Yangtze River Estuary Were Transferred to the Front Lines. It is Reported that the Japanese Troops Stationed in Zhudi Have Withdrawn 77

The English-language "Great American Evening Post" reported that, according to reliable sources, the Japanese army suffered heavy casualties in its brutal anti-guerrilla warfare in western Shanghai. The guerrillas, because the Japanese army massacred villagers and burned villages, bravely came forward to retaliate. With the help of the peasants, they counterattacked the Japanese army in various places. Their actions were swift and flexible, and it is said that they have achieved significant victories. On Sunday and Monday, a team of Japanese troops was cut off by guerrillas in the Songzhu area of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway and suffered a heavy blow. The Japanese army urgently dispatched a large increase in troops, resulting in the area being filled with Japanese troops in some places. In recent months, the number of Japanese troops stationed in most towns along the Yangtze River has been greatly reduced, because most of them have been sent to the front lines for reinforcement, and have been transferred to the "Peace and National Salvation Army" to show non-assistance. Since the outbreak of large-scale guerrilla warfare, the Japanese army in central China has been exhausted and feels a great lack of manpower. Although the Japanese army has destroyed villages and towns on a large scale in an attempt to eliminate the base areas of the guerrillas, the guerrillas continue to operate. On Tuesday evening, the Japanese side sent several ambulances to the North Station to pick up the wounded Japanese soldiers from the guerrilla area.

Withdrawal of Japanese Troops

On the 26th of last month, about 1,000 Japanese troops went to the towns of Zhudi, Panlong, Jiwangmiao, and Guanyintang in western Shanghai and were stationed separately in these places. It is now reported that yesterday (the 1st), about 200 Japanese troops stationed in Zhudi forcibly gathered all the residents of the town in one place. Those who were afraid and avoided were beaten. After the Japanese puppet leaders gave "comforting speeches" to the gathered residents, the Japanese troops immediately withdrew to Shanghai. It is said that the Japanese troops stationed in other towns will also withdraw in the near future.

On-Site Inspection

The "Continental News" reported that Qingpu District, five miles west of Shanghai, has recently been poisoned by the Japanese army. On Sunday, five British and American journalists from this city went to the area to investigate and witnessed twelve villages burned to the ground and injured and killed villagers. The heart-wrenching scenes and photos of the burned villages have all been published in the "Continental News". The spokesperson of the Japanese Army in this city yesterday (the 1st) denied burning more than one village and killing women and children.

Covering Up the Facts

It is said that Qingpu District is a nest of Communist guerrillas, and the anti-Japanese sentiment is extremely strong. Moreover, guerrillas disguised as villagers killed several Japanese soldiers. A team of Japanese troops began military operations against the guerrillas on April 14, with the aim of completely eliminating the Communist elements. The Japanese army conducted household searches and found many Communist elements disguised as farmers, and seized a large number of military weapons and ammunition. The Japanese army acted with extreme caution, so the claim in the anti-Japanese newspapers that civilians, including women and children, were killed is not true. There was only one village that caught fire, and the guerrillas who killed the Japanese soldiers had their headquarters in the village.

Raising Funds for Burial

Now there are seventeen people, including Zhang Jinxiang, who have launched a campaign to raise funds to bury the exposed corpses. The notice says: What is more heartbreaking in the world than dying without a burial place and exposing bones in the wilderness? Those who suffer may be unaware in the underworld, but how can those who see it not feel pain in their hearts? This time, the northern countryside of Sijing Town suffered a tragic massacre by a certain army, which has been recorded in various newspapers. Innocent farmers have suffered this great calamity, corpses are everywhere, and the stench is overwhelming. Is there no danger of causing an epidemic? Jinxiang and others, in view of this, will rush to collect and bury the corpses everywhere as soon as possible, but the cost is very high. Feeling inadequate, we have to widely solicit donations. If so, the ownerless lonely souls will suffer less from the dismemberment of corpses, and the common people in the wilderness will not suffer from the disaster of the epidemic. This is a win-win situation. If benevolent people are willing to donate generously, then not only will the dead receive great kindness, but the living will also receive infinite blessings. This is an appeal. Also, the previous report that Magistrate Lu of Qingpu County led his troops to surrender to the puppet regime has been corrected by the county government, which stated that it was completely untrue.

Hu Siting Was Shot Dead. It Is Reported that There Was a Nature of Revenge, Involving the Bloodshed at the Wangjiasha Law School. It is Said that Hu Once Sniped Chen Jinbiao 78

At No. 1081 Jing'an Temple Road, Daxia University, at about 1:08 p.m. the day before yesterday, a sudden assassination occurred. The person shot was Hu Siting from Kunshan, 19 years old, a freshman in the law department of the school. He was hit by two bullets in the chest on the spot and died immediately. All the details have been recorded in the newspapers.

One Person Was Detained, Also a Student

According to Pingming News Agency reporters, after Hu fell to the ground after being shot, the shooter sneaked out of the school gate and fled along Jing'an Temple Road. At that time, he did not hide or abandon the gun he was holding. Two Chinese constables, No. 58 and No. 134, saw him and immediately pursued him, and as a result, they arrested the assassin and detained him in the Jing'an Temple Police Station, and then escorted him to the Central Police Station on Simalu. The pistol and bullet casings were also sent to the General Police Station for examination. It is said that the assassin is also a young man, one of the students of Daxia University, named Chen Yiping (but inquiries with the school authorities deny that there is such a student). The motive for the assassination is said to be revenge. The reason is that Hu Siting shot Chen Jinbiao, a student of the Shanghai Law School, on Aivenyi Road in the Wangjiasha Garden on April 12. He and Chen were close friends, and being moved by righteousness, he could not let him survive, so on that day he walked from Jing'an Temple Road into the Daxia school building and shot Hu directly. He did not give any verbal warnings beforehand. Currently, the police station is investigating the deceased Hu Siting's past political activities at the school and his relationship to the Wangjiasha bloodshed.

The Deceased's Unusual Activities on Weekdays

Hu Siting's father, named Wenkai, has been an editor at the Commercial Press, earning only a few dozen yuan a month, and his family is poor, so he lives very frugally. It is said that the son used to rent a room in a building on Aiduya Road under the name of the Sichuan Fellow Association as a cover, and internally specialized in a certain kind of work. Later, it moved to Cishu Building and was renamed the Shanghai Jiangbian Compilation and Translation Society. It held meetings once a week from 7 to 9 p.m. every Saturday. In the past, Hu also served the Party and the country and embraced the Three Principles of the People, but suddenly changed his attitude and secretly engaged in unusual activities.

The kidnapped were Feng Yunji (38 years old), a Shaoxing native of the Nanyang Tobacco Company, who lived at No. 23 Chengxing Lane, Parker Road, Public Concession, and Li Zitang (40 years old), a Guangdong native, who lived at No. 143 Pupo Lane, Luban Road, French Concession. Feng is currently the director of the tobacco leaf department of the company, and Li is the director of the cigarette packing department. At that time, when Feng and Li were passing in front of the Taichang Woodware Company, suddenly five bandits, each with a pistol, searched them. The two were forced into a car parked on the side of the road, number one two four (owned by Tailai Automobile Company), and sped west. Afterwards, after someone reported the case, the Jing'an Temple Police Station sent Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to investigate everything in detail. The reason why Feng and Li were kidnapped is still under investigation by the police.

Lin Daosheng Was Also Kidnapped

Lin Daosheng from Wuxi went to the Xiqing Pool at No. 556 Jiujiang Road alone at 6:10 p.m. yesterday to take a bath. When Lin was undressing to enter the pool, suddenly three thugs rushed to Lin, threatening him with pistols and telling him to get dressed. When Lin Daosheng saw the pistols, he dared not resist, and was taken out by the thugs and boarded a silver car (registration number 8267) parked on the side of the road and sped away. Afterwards, the police station in charge of the area received a report and sent detectives to investigate. As for the reason why Lin was kidnapped, the police are still investigating. It is said that Lin Daosheng came to Shanghai from Wuxi only yesterday.

Four Gambling Dens in Shanghai Xi Were Closed Down Yesterday 84

The saying that Shanghai Xi gambling dens would be banned has long been rumored. Although a number of casinos, such as Guangsheng, Shenji, Xiangsheng, Rend, Jing'an, and Zhuan, were closed down last month, the larger ones were still operating as usual, and their business was more prosperous than before. Therefore, the small gambling dens that were closed down were actively discussing ways to deal with the situation and trying to resume business, but the Japanese side has not yet given a definite reply. On the morning of the day before yesterday (May 1), the director of the "Gambling Den Supervision Department", Yamaki, and the Chinese "chief in charge", Pan Sansheng, ordered four casinos, including Fusheng, Dasheng, Lianyi (that is, Kai Xile), and Xinxin, to close down. It is said that the owner of Fusheng is more flexible in his methods. It is said that he will resume business in four days, but according to news from the Japanese side, the existing casinos such as Hollywood have also been ordered to suspend operations within a certain period of time. As for the "Chinese General Association" in Jing'an Temple, because of its special license, the "Department" has no right to deal with it. It is said that it can be extended for six months.

Gambling Dens in Nanshi Are Plotting a Revival 85

A large number of gambling dens in Nanshi were banned by the Japanese military police because of a bloody incident in the Heng'an gambling den in Heng'an Lane. It is now known that the ashes have been re-ignited and are plotting a revival, because large gambling dens such as Sanxin on Minguo Road have spent a huge amount of capital, so it is no small matter to try. Therefore, in the bustling areas around the refugee area, there are 14 gambling dens preparing to appear in a new guise and have been successfully dredged. Suicide and Miscellaneous Records: A Woman's Bizarre Death, Double Suicide Attempt with Poison, One Dead, One Critical 86

Local woman Cao, aged 30, together with a man named Cao Zitian, aged 35, claiming to be her husband, arrived at the Da Fang Hotel at 35 Zhengjia Wood Bridge Street in the French Concession at 11:00 AM on the 30th of last month. They booked room 216 for lodging. At 2:00 PM, the man and woman went out together and returned to the hotel around 6:00 PM in the evening to sleep. The next morning around 6:00 AM, the man Cao Zitian went out alone, leaving the woman inside. She slept until 11:00 AM at noon and had not gotten up. The tea server Xu Dingchang (22 years old, from Ningbo) entered the room to inquire and discovered that Ms. Cao had died in bed. He immediately informed the accounting office, which reported to the French police. Detectives were dispatched to investigate and found what appeared to be strangulation marks on the deceased's neck and her fingernails were blue. The cause of death was unclear, so the body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan branch morgue for examination. Yesterday, Prosecutor Zhao Changmin from the Special No. 2 Court was requested to come to the morgue to conduct an examination. The examination revealed that Cao had died of poison before her death. Because there was no way to find or summon her family, the official determined that the corpse should be handled by the charity for burial, pending family identification. However, the man who stayed with her, Cao Zitian, claiming to be her husband, did not return to the hotel. It is said that the police department dispatched detectives to investigate and investigate the cause of the woman's suicide. Zhang Yuansheng (28 years old) and his wife Zhang Wang (26 years old), arrived at the China Hotel at 241 Jie Road in the Public Concession at about 4 PM the day before yesterday. They booked room number 5 for lodging. Yesterday, at 11:15 AM, the tea waiter heard moaning from the room. He went to knock on the door, but there was no answer. He managed to pry open the door and saw Zhang and his wife lying on the bed with pale faces, moaning, and barely conscious. He saw an empty bottle of poisonous liquid on the table, indicating that they had taken poison. He immediately reported to the accounting office and summoned an ambulance to take the couple to the hospital for treatment. Zhang Yuansheng died of poisoning before reaching the hospital. Wang's life is also in critical condition. It is said that the reason for the suicide was economic pressure.

Pan Xiang, a young man from Suzhou, age 24, residing at 10 Bie Mo (phonetic) Ten Garden on Long Road, had just graduated from school last year during the winter vacation. He had been suffering from lung disease for four years. He had sought medical treatment repeatedly, even having his kidney removed, but none of the medicines were effective. He felt no joy in life and the future was bleak, so he held a pessimistic view. On the 29th of last month, he suddenly became desperate. That night, at 10:00 PM, he secretly swallowed poison at home to commit suicide. His mother discovered it and searched his bedside and found sleeping pills and an empty iodine bottle. He was immediately sent to Renji Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and he died at 2:00 PM on the 1st of this month.

Chen Jingying (29 years old), a Fujian woman, residing at 45 Jianye Lane, Fulili Road, had an argument with her husband at 8:00 PM last night. Afterwards, she swallowed raw opium to commit suicide. Her family discovered it and sent her to the hospital for treatment.

Yesterday, at 2:00 PM, a traveler, Zhang Weixin (20 years old), a local man in Room 213 of the Continental Hotel on Yü Qiaqing Road, jumped from a second-floor window, attempting suicide due to economic pressure. He fell onto the sidewalk and suffered severe injuries to his head. He was then taken to the hospital by ambulance, and his life may be in danger.

Sad Story of a Young Woman: Young Widow Subjected to Abuse by Step-Aunt, Attempted Joint Suicide with Daughter Unsuccessful, Spared Punishment 89

Yan Zhong, the daughter of Zhong Lu, a woman from Suzhou residing at No. 2, Lane 181, Xiaoshadu Road, 27 years old, was married eight years ago by her parents, through a matchmaker, to Zhi Qian (the son of Yan Jia Zhuo, Zi Junshu, the former Director of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office (i.e., the offspring of Yan Jiachi, Zi Mengfan, the former Director of the Jiangsu Finance Department of the Beijing Government and now the Vice Minister of Finance of the "Central Government" in Nanjing). She lived together at No. 25, Meilefang, Lane 210, Huanlong Road in the French Concession. However, since Yan Zhong married into the family, she has suffered greatly from abuse from her step-aunt and being in an old-fashioned family. Furthermore, her husband was studying at Soochow University in Suzhou, and he was unable to protect her. Unexpectedly, Zhi Qian became weak and went to Peking Union Medical College Hospital for treatment. He repeatedly sent letters to summon his wife to Beijing, but was blocked by his parents. It was not until Zhi Qian was terminally ill that Zhong was able to rush to his bedside. After a brief reunion, he died. At that time, Ms. Zhong's nerves were severely stimulated and she once jumped from the second floor in an attempt to commit suicide. She was rescued and spared from death. When she returned to Shanghai with the coffin, she was refused by her parents. Ms. Zhong took her daughter Qingyi (now eight years old) to Ningbo temporarily to live. It has been more than four years and her parents have not expressed any intention to take her back. She once requested living expenses from her parents and filed a lawsuit in the Suzhou court. The first instance ruled that she could receive more than 3,000 yuan in living expenses, but she lost the appeal. The case is now delayed in the Supreme Court. Ms. Yan comes from a well-known family, knows etiquette, and has received higher education. Being a young widow is already a tragedy in life. Being abandoned by her parents is even more painful. She has been living in Ningbo for four years. Although her parents have no complaints, she feels ashamed to live there for a long time when she occasionally thinks of the old etiquette of "a married daughter is like spilled water". She has no joy in life and nothing to look forward to. In a state of depression, she had suicidal thoughts. On April 26, at 5 PM, Ms. Zhong and her eight-year-old daughter Qingyi simultaneously swallowed three bottles of sleeping pills to commit suicide. Fortunately, the family discovered it early and sent them to the Red Cross Hospital for emergency treatment. The mother and daughter survived. The Jing'an Temple Police Station was notified and sent Detective Xie Futang to investigate. Because she had attempted to kill her daughter, Yan Zhong was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the Special First Court yesterday morning. The police initially charged her with murder under Article 271, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. After questioning by Judge Fu, Yan Zhong confessed that she often kept sleeping pills because she suffered from insomnia after her husband's death. She had not forced her daughter to take poison and Yan Qingyi also testified that she had taken it herself. Under the defense of lawyer Wang Jianhang, police lawyer Zhang Tianyin also stated that he should be judged in accordance with Article 275 of the Criminal Law for attempting to commit joint suicide. Judge Fu reviewed the confession and sentenced Yan Zhong to be exempt from punishment for attempting to commit joint suicide and inciting suicide. Qingyi was taken back by her maternal grandmother.

Case of Wu Qilun's Murder: Gu Zhuxuan Denies Instigation, All Criminals Have Confessed in the Police Station, Confession Forms Submitted to the Court, Gu Denies the Matter Outright, Adjournment Ordered for Further Investigation 90

The case of Gu Zhuxuan being accused of instigating the murder of lawyer Wu Qilun was heard in the Criminal Court One by Judge Feng Shide of the Special First Court yesterday afternoon. Gu's lawyers Wu Linkun, Jiang Baoli, Jiang Pingfan, and Qiao Yaoshan's lawyer Wang Yaofa were all present in court. First, police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated: The defendants related to the case of Wu Qilun's murder are Wei Shoulin, Wang Xingfang, Xia Shoufeng, Xia Guifu, Zeng Changchun, Qiao Yaoshan, and Gu Zhuxuan, a total of seven people. They are now being prosecuted in accordance with Article 171 of the Criminal Law. Gu Zhuxuan and Wu Qilun were acquainted and very friendly. Previously, Gu's apprentice Wang Xinggao killed Tang Jiapeng, and was arrested by the French police. Gu was also arrested for his involvement in instigating the crime. At that time, Wu Qilun was his lawyer. Afterwards, Gu expressed dissatisfaction because Wu had not done his best. Later, Wu represented Qiu Changyin in a guardianship case. As a result, the case was settled through Gu's mediation. Qiu sent a public fee of 30,000 yuan, but Gu did not share the money with Wu, causing Wu to complain. Gu hated Wu to the core because Wu publicized the matter, which affected his reputation. He discussed with his apprentice Qiao Yaoshan how to kill Wu. Qiao then contacted Zeng Changchun, and then successively found Wei Shoulin, Wang Xingfang, Xia Shoufeng, Xia Guifu, Wei Xiaohu (who was killed by the police in another theft case), and others. After discussion, they decided on a method to kill Wu Qilun and designated Xia Guifu as the executor. However, all the defendants did not know Wu Qilun's true face. Therefore, they sent Zeng to accompany Wei and Xia to visit Wu at his residence at No. 102, Tongfu Road, to handle the defense of Ding Shaokun (who had been arrested by the police for robbery and sentenced by the court). After Xia recognized Wu's face, they agreed to pay 100 yuan in public fees on the morning of March 4. That morning at 11:30, Wei Xiaohu, disguised as a rickshaw puller, pulled an empty rickshaw with a pistol borrowed from a certain organization in Shanghai West (the gun had been used in many cases in the concession). They set off together. After arriving at the destination, Wei handed the gun to Xia Guifu, who went to knock on the door, while the others were distributed to watch the wind. When Xia knocked on the door, Wu Qilun thought that someone was coming to pay the public fee, so he ordered his niece Wu Shaohua to open the door and invite the person into the living room. After only a few words, Xia took out the gun and fired three shots at Wu and fled. Wu died because the bullets hit vital parts. In the beginning, Gu was supposed to pay 2,000 yuan as a reward after the deed was done, but only paid 800 yuan. These facts were all confessed by the defendants, and the confession forms have been made. However, Gu Zhuxuan denied everything in the police station. Therefore, the confession forms were submitted to the court. Then, Wu Shaohua testified about the circumstances of Xia Guifu firing the gun at the time. Judge Feng often questioned Xia Guifu, Wei Shoulin, Wang Xingfang, and Zeng Changchun, and they all admitted to the fact of killing Wu without denying it. By this time, it was already dusk, so the court announced an adjournment for further questioning.

Fire in Nanshi: Five Houses Burned, Two People Injured in Falls 91

At No. 65, Xue Lane, West of the Sanpailou (Three Memorial Archways) in the city, a three-story house, the tenant Li Amao (from Pudong), who traded in foreign jadeite, had an argument with his wife around 8:50 PM the night before last. They were later taken to the refugee hospital by ambulance for treatment. The fire department dispatched vehicles from the Northern District Fire Brigade to put out the fire. It took about two hours to extinguish the fire. Five houses were burned in this fire.

Letter 96

To the Editor, We write to inform you that, according to Mr. Liu Huilin of Liu Yanghe Tang Traditional Chinese Medicine Shop, upon reading the news about the fire in Ningxing Street, French Concession, i.e., the Caishi (Vegetable Market) Street, published in your newspaper yesterday, he was greatly surprised that the statements made were inconsistent with the facts. Our shop has been located near Gaochang Temple in Nanshi for over 60 years after moving to the French Concession after the war. The report that our shop was originally located in Hongkou and moved to Caishi Street after August 13th is obviously hearsay and untrue. It is also untrue that the fire was caused by our shop accidentally burning ointment in the kitchen. Our shop usually closes at 9:30 PM every night and turns off the lights at 10:00 PM, so how could such an ointment burning event occur? Furthermore, the report that our shop has huge fire insurance is also inconsistent with the facts. Our shop has capital of more than 20,000 yuan, while the fire insurance is only 3,000 yuan, which is a far cry. The loss is quite large, so how can it be said that we have huge fire insurance? Also, the tenants of the second and third floors of the building leased by our shop, Dong and Bao, directly lease from the landlord Siming Real Estate Department. The report that these tenants sublet from our shop is obviously untrue. We are deeply concerned that this untrue news will lead to misunderstandings from all parties, and we have to entrust your lawyer to send a letter to Shen Bao and Xin Bao to declare a correction. We hereby forward the letter and request your newspaper to make a correction. Sincerely, Lawyer Jiang Chiping, May 2nd.
